## <a name="windows-server-2008-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="631fb-810">Atributos do Windows Server 2008</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="631fb-810">Windows Server 2008 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="631fb-811">Essa classe contém os seguintes atributos para o Windows Server 2008:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="631fb-811">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2008:</span></span>
